ASCII Addition

Nowadays, there are smartphone applications that instantly translate text and even solve math problems if you just point your phone’s camera at them. Your job is to implement a much simpler functionality reminiscent of the past – add two integers written down as ASCII art.

An ASCII art is a matrix of characters, exactly 77 rows high, with each individual character either a dot or the lowercase letter x.

An expression of the form a+ba+b is given, where both aa and bb are positive integers. The expression is converted into ASCII art by writing all the expression characters (the digits of aa and bb as well as the + sign) as 7×57×5 matrices, and concatenating the matrices together with a single column of dot characters between consecutive individual matrices. The exact matrices corresponding to the digits and the + sign are as folows:

xxxxx
x...x
x...x
x...x
x...x
x...x
xxxxx

....x
....x
....x
....x
....x

....x

xxxxx

xxxxx

xxxxx

..x..

..x..

.....

Given an ASCII art for an expression of the form a+ba+b, find the result of the addition and write it out in the ASCII art form.

Input

Input consists of exactly 77 lines and contains the ASCII art for an expression of the form a+ba+b, where both aa and bb are positive integers consisting of at most 99 decimal digits and written without leading zeros.

Output

Output 77 lines containing ASCII art corresponding to the result of the addition, without leading zeros.

Sample Input 1 Sample Output 1 
....x.xxxxx.xxxxx.x...x.xxxxx.xxxxx.xxxxx.......xxxxx.xxxxx.xxxxx
....x.....x.....x.x...x.x.....x.........x...x...x...x.x...x.x...x
....x.....x.....x.x...x.x.....x.........x...x...x...x.x...x.x...x
....x.xxxxx.xxxxx.xxxxx.xxxxx.xxxxx.....x.xxxxx.xxxxx.xxxxx.x...x
....x.x.........x.....x.....x.x...x.....x...x...x...x.....x.x...x
....x.x.........x.....x.....x.x...x.....x...x...x...x.....x.x...x
....x.xxxxx.xxxxx.....x.xxxxx.xxxxx.....x.......xxxxx.xxxxx.xxxxx

....x.xxxxx.xxxxx.xxxxx.x...x.xxxxx.xxxxx

....x.x.........x.....x.....x.....x.....x
